<script type="text/javascript">
    window.addEventListener('scroll', unmissableOnScroll);
    function unmissableOnScroll() {
        var yOffset = window.pageYOffset;
        var topDiv = document.getElementById("ad-unit-unmissable-top-sticky-banner");
        if(topDiv && yOffset > 900){
            var position = 0 - (yOffset-900);
            if(position < -50){
                closeUnmissable(true);
                window.scrollBy(0, -50);
            }
        }
    };
    
    const unmissableCookieName = "unmissableIsClosed";
    var isUnmissable = false;

    function setClass(searchClass, addClass) {
        $.each($(searchClass),
            function () {
                $(this).addClass(addClass);
            });
    }

    function removeClass(searchClass, className) {
        $.each($(searchClass),
            function () {
                $(this).removeClass(className);
            });
    }

    $(document).ready(function () {
        if (document.cookie.indexOf(unmissableCookieName) === -1) {
            window.googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                window.googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotOnload',
                    function (event) {
                        var slot = event.slot;
                        var slotId = slot.getSlotElementId();
    
                        if (slotId === "gam_unmissable_pos_top_sticky_banner") {
                            removeClass(".has-mega-nav.unmissable", "unmissable");
                        }
                    });
    
                window.googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded',
                    function (event) {
                        var slot = event.slot;
                        var slotId = slot.getSlotElementId();
    
                        if (slotId === "gam_unmissable_pos_top_sticky_banner" && !event.isEmpty) {
                            isUnmissable = true;
                            setClass(".has-mega-nav", "unmissable");
                            setClass(".compare-panel.close-panel", "unmissable");
                            setClass(".site-nav-wrapper.csn-theme", "unmissable");
                            setClass(".header-sticky.header-meganav", "unmissable");
                            setClass(".header", "unmissable");
                            setClass(".csn-theme.site-nav-wrapper .site-nav", "unmissable");
                            setClass(".header.reset-header", "unmissable");
                            setClass(".header-sticky.reset", "unmissable");
                            setClass(".sticky-top.sidebar-mega-nav", "unmissable");
                            document.getElementById("close-button-container").style.display = "flex";
                        }
                    });
            });
        }
    });
    function closeUnmissable(autoClosed) {
        removeClass(".has-mega-nav", "unmissable");
        removeClass(".compare-panel.close-panel", "unmissable");
        removeClass(".site-nav-wrapper.csn-theme", "unmissable");
        removeClass(".header-sticky.header-meganav", "unmissable");
        removeClass(".header", "unmissable");
        removeClass(".csn-theme.site-nav-wrapper .site-nav", "unmissable");
        removeClass(".header.reset-header", "unmissable");
        removeClass(".header-sticky.reset", "unmissable");
        removeClass(".sticky-top.sidebar-mega-nav", "unmissable");
        
        var unmissableBanner = document.getElementById("ad-unit-unmissable-top-sticky-banner");
        unmissableBanner.remove();
        if(!autoClosed){
            if (decodeURIComponent(document.cookie).indexOf(unmissableCookieName) === -1) {
                var date = new Date();
                var midnight = new Date(date.getFullYear(), date.getMonth(), date.getDate(), 23, 59, 59);
                var expires = "expires="+ midnight.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = unmissableCookieName + "=1;" + expires + ";path=/";

                    url:"https://pubads.g.doubleclick.net/gampad/clk?id=5675485371&iu=/21842759191",
                    crossDomain: true,
                    dataType: 'jsonp',
                });
            }
        }
    }

<script>

    window.CsnInsights = window.CsnInsights || {};

    CsnInsights.Constants = {
        dealerValues: ['dealer', 'agencia', 'industry dealer'],
        privateSellerValues: ['private', 'particular'],
        tkappname: "carsales-desktop"
    };
    CsnInsights.CookieHelper = {
        set: function (cname, cvalue, exdays, domain='') {
            if (exdays > 0) {
                var d = new Date();
                d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();
                document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
            }
            else {
                if (domain !== '') {
                    var d = new Date();
                    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (1 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                    var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();
                    document.cookie = cname + '=' + cvalue + ';domain=' + domain + ';path=/';
                }
                else {
                    document.cookie = cname + '=' + cvalue + ';path=/';
                }
            }
        },
        get: function (cname) {
            var name = cname + "=";
            var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
            var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
            for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                var c = ca[i];
                while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                    c = c.substring(1);
                }
                if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                    return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
                }
            }
            return "";
        }
    };
    CsnInsights.StringHelper = {
        append_with_comma: function (v, appto) {
            if ((appto || '') !== '') {
                return v + ',' + appto
            }
            return v
        }
    };
    CsnInsights.GuidHelper = {
        build: function () {
            function s4() {
                return Math.floor((1 + Math.random()) * 0x10000)
                    .toString(16)
                    .substring(1);
            }
            return s4() + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' +
                s4() + '-' + s4() + s4() + s4();
        },
        buildV2: function () {
            return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function (c) {
                var r = Math.random() * 16 | 0, v = c == 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3 | 0x8);
                return v.toString(16);
            });
        }
    };

    CsnInsights.LoadEventId = CsnInsights.GuidHelper.build();        

    CsnInsights.CurrentClient = {
        sessionKey: "csn.bi",        
        getId: function () {
            var key = "csnclientid";
            var versionKey = "cidgenerated";
            var currentUserId = (CsnInsights.CookieHelper.get(key) || '');
            var generatedVersion = (CsnInsights.CookieHelper.get(versionKey) || '').toString();

            var domain = window.location.hostname;
            var duplicateDomain = '.' + domain;
            var appName = CsnInsights.Constants.tkappname;

            if ((generatedVersion === 'client' || generatedVersion === '1') && (currentUserId || "") != "") {
                return currentUserId;
            }
            else {
                if (currentUserId !== '') {
                    CsnInsights.CookieHelper.set("p_csnclientid", currentUserId, 5 * 365);
                }
                userId1 = CsnInsights.GuidHelper.build();
                userId2 = CsnInsights.GuidHelper.buildV2();
                newUserId = (userId1 + '-' + userId2 + '-' + (new Date).getTime().toString()).toUpperCase();
                if (generatedVersion === '' && currentUserId !== '' && (appName === 'carsales-desktop' || appName === 'carsales-mobi')) {
                    CsnInsights.CookieHelper.set(key, newUserId, 0, duplicateDomain);
                }
                CsnInsights.CookieHelper.set(key, newUserId, 5 * 365);
                CsnInsights.CookieHelper.set(versionKey, 'client', 5 * 365);           
                return newUserId;
            }
        },
        getCidGenerated: function () {
            var key = "cidgenerated";
            var cidGenerated = CsnInsights.CookieHelper.get(key);
            return cidGenerated;
        },
        getPrevId: function () {
            var key = "csnclientid";
            var prevKey = "p_csnclientid";
            var prevUserId = (CsnInsights.CookieHelper.get(prevKey) || '');
            var newUserId = CsnInsights.CookieHelper.get(key);

            if (prevUserId !== '') {
                if (prevUserId !== newUserId) {
                    return prevUserId;
                }
            }
            else {
                return '';
            }
        },
        getDomain: function () {
            return window.location
        },
        getA360Id: function () {
            var thirtyMinsInDay = 0.020833333;
            var key = "a360Fb"; /* For backword compatibility we keep the name same */
            var a360FbId = CsnInsights.CookieHelper.get("a360Fb");

            if (!a360FbId) {
                xmlHttp = new XMLHttpRequest();

                if (xmlHttp != null) {           
                    try {
                        xmlHttp.open('GET', 'https://a360cdn.azureedge.net/javascript/a360.consent.default.js', false);
                        xmlHttp.send(null);

                        if (xmlHttp.status === 200) {
                            a360FbId = 'true';
                            CsnInsightsHelper.setCookie('a360Fb', 'true', thirtyMinsInDay);                   
                        }
                        else {
                            a360FbId = 'false';
                            CsnInsightsHelper.setCookie('a360Fb', 'false', thirtyMinsInDay);
                        }
                    } catch (e) { }
                }
            }
            return a360FbId;
        },
        extendA360IdExpiry: function () {
            var key = "a360Fb";
            var thirtyMinsInDay = 0.020833333;
            var a360FbId = CsnInsights.CookieHelper.get("a360Fb");

            if (!a360FbId) {
                CsnInsights.CurrentClient.getA360Id();
            }
            else {
                CsnInsights.CookieHelper.set(key, a360FbId, thirtyMinsInDay);
            }
            return a360FbId;
        },
        getSessionId: function () {
            var thirtyMinsInDay = 0.020833333;
            var key = CsnInsights.CurrentClient.sessionKey; /* For backword compatibility we keep the name same */
            var currentSessionId = CsnInsights.CookieHelper.get("csn.bi");

            if (!currentSessionId) {
                currentSessionId = (new Date).getTime().toString();
                CsnInsights.CookieHelper.set(key, currentSessionId, thirtyMinsInDay );
            }
            return currentSessionId;
        },
        extendSessionIdExpiry: function () {
            var key = CsnInsights.CurrentClient.sessionKey; 
            var thirtyMinsInDay = 0.020833333;
            var currentSessionId = CsnInsights.CookieHelper.get("csn.bi");

            if (!currentSessionId) {
                CsnInsights.CurrentClient.getSessionId();
            }
            else {
                CsnInsights.CookieHelper.set(key, currentSessionId, thirtyMinsInDay);                
            }
            return currentSessionId;
        }
    };
    var t_csncid = CsnInsights.CurrentClient.getId();
    var t_csnbi = CsnInsights.CurrentClient.extendSessionIdExpiry();
    var t_a360Fb = CsnInsights.CurrentClient.extendA360IdExpiry();
    


            CsnInsights.geoCountryCode = "AU";
        
</script>

<script>
    window.CsnInsights = window.CsnInsights || {};

    window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper = {
        sdkNseNo: 0,

        assetId: function (metaData) {
            if (typeof metaData === 'undefined') return 'none';

            var result = '';
            if (((metaData.contentgroup1 || metaData.contentGroup1) ===
                (metaData.contentgroup2 || metaData.contentGroup2))
                || (metaData.area === (metaData.pagetype || metaData.pageType))) {
                result = (metaData.contentgroup1 || metaData.contentGroup1 || metaData.area || '').toLowerCase().replace(/( |_)/g, '-');
            } else {
                result = (((metaData.contentgroup1 || metaData.contentGroup1 || metaData.area || '') + '-' +
                    (metaData.contentgroup2 || metaData.contentGroup2 || metaData.pagetype || metaData.pageType || location.pathname))).toLowerCase().replace(/( |_)/g, '-');
            }
            return result;
        },
        url_rp: function (metaData, overridePageUrl) {
            return 'page_' + window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.assetId(metaData || window.CsnInsights.metaData) + '_' + location.origin + overridePageUrl;
        },
        segB: function (metaData) {
            if (typeof metaData === 'undefined') return '';
            if (((metaData.contentgroup1 || metaData.contentGroup1 || metaData.area || '').toLowerCase() === 'news and reviews') ||
                ((metaData.contentgroup1 || metaData.contentGroup1 || metaData.area || '').toLowerCase() === 'profile-pages') ||
                (window.location.hostname.includes('carsales') &&
                (metaData.contentgroup1 || metaData.contentGroup1 || metaData.area || '').toLowerCase() === 'showroom')) {
                return 'carsales - news, reviews and content';
            }
        },
        subbrand: function (metaData) {
            if (typeof metaData === 'undefined') return '';
            if (((metaData.contentgroup1 || metaData.contentGroup1 || metaData.area || '').toLowerCase() === 'news and reviews') ||
                ((metaData.contentgroup1 || metaData.contentGroup1 || metaData.area || '').toLowerCase() === 'profile-pages') ||
                (window.location.hostname.includes('carsales') &&
                ((metaData.contentgroup1 || metaData.contentGroup1 || metaData.area || '').toLowerCase() === 'showroom')) &&
                ('' !== '')) {
                return '';
            }
            else return '';
        },
        /*added below to check if editorial or not */
        appId: function (metaData) {
            if (typeof metaData === 'undefined') return 'P0F76F26B-7820-43C1-A19C-00FF9A986EBD';
            if (((metaData.contentgroup1 || metaData.contentGroup1 || metaData.area || '').toLowerCase() === 'news and reviews') ||
                ((metaData.contentgroup1 || metaData.contentGroup1 || metaData.area || '').toLowerCase() === 'profile-pages') ||
                (window.location.hostname.includes('carsales') &&
                ((metaData.contentgroup1 || metaData.contentGroup1 || metaData.area || '').toLowerCase() === 'showroom')) &&
                ('P14C4BEF5-18CE-44C0-8B5C-6E90BC08AD9B' !== '')) {
                return 'P14C4BEF5-18CE-44C0-8B5C-6E90BC08AD9B';
            }
            else return 'P0F76F26B-7820-43C1-A19C-00FF9A986EBD';
        },
        getTargetId: function () {
            return 1;
        },
        sendEvent: function (eventContextmetaData, eventCategory, eventLabel, eventAction, overridePageUrl, variantTestContext) {

            if (nSdkInstance) {
                if ((eventContextmetaData.contentgroup2 || eventContextmetaData.contentGroup2 || eventContextmetaData.pageType || eventContextmetaData.pagetype).toLowerCase() === 'gallery') {
                    if (eventAction === "swipe") {
                        indexVal = (eventLabel || 1)

                        window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.sdkNseNo = ++window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.sdkNseNo;
                        nSdkInstance.ggPM("onPaginate", { "eventType": "slide", "descriptor": indexVal});
                                            }
                }                
            } 
                    },
        sendPageView: function (eventContextmetaData, overridePageUrl) {

            if (window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.trac) {
                /*window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper
                     .trac['referrer'] = window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.trac.customReferrer || document.referrer;
                     */
                window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.trac['page_url'] = location.origin + overridePageUrl;
                if (overridePageUrl) {

                    if (window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.trac.customReferrer) {
                        window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.trac.pageEvent(window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.assetId(eventContextmetaData || window.CsnInsights.metaData));
                    } else {

                        window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.trac.post();
                    }

                    window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.trac.customReferrer = window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.url_rp(eventContextmetaData, overridePageUrl) ;

                } else {
                    window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.trac['page_url'] = window.location.href;
                    window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.trac.post();
                    window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.trac.customReferrer = window.location.href;
                }
            }


                var referrerUrl;
            if (window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.myDcrMetadata) {
                nSdkInstance.ggPM("staticend", window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.myDcrMetadata);
                referrerUrl = window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.myDcrMetadata.pageURL;
            }
            if (window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.subbrand != null && window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.subbrand != '') {
                window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.myDcrMetadata = {
                    type: "static",
                    dataSrc: "cms",
                    assetid: window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.assetId(eventContextmetaData || window.CsnInsights.metaData),

                    section: "carsales.com.au - brand only",
                    segA: "carsales - automotive",
                    segB: window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.segB(eventContextmetaData || window.CsnInsights.metaData),
                    subbrand: window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.subbrand(eventContextmetaData || window.CsnInsights.metaData)
                };
            }
            else {
                window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.myDcrMetadata = {
                    type: "static",
                    dataSrc: "cms",
                    assetid: window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.assetId(eventContextmetaData || window.CsnInsights.metaData),

                    section: "carsales.com.au - brand only",
                    segA: "carsales - automotive",
                    segB: window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.segB(eventContextmetaData || window.CsnInsights.metaData)
                };
            }
                if (referrerUrl) {
                    window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.myDcrMetadata.referrerURL = referrerUrl;
                }
                if (overridePageUrl) {
                    /*window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.myDcrMetadata.pageURL = overridePageUrl;*/
                    window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.myDcrMetadata.pageURL
                        = 'page_' + window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.assetId(eventContextmetaData || window.CsnInsights.metaData) + '_' + location.origin + overridePageUrl;
                }

                nSdkInstance.ggPM("staticstart", window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.myDcrMetadata);

            
        }
    };

        function NielsenTracker() {

                sendPageView: function (eventContextmetaData, overridePageUrl, variantTestContext) {
                    window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.sendPageView(eventContextmetaData, overridePageUrl);

                },
                getTargetId: function () {
                    return window.CsnInsights.NielsenHelper.getTargetId();
                }
            };
        }
        window.NielsenTracker = window.NielsenTracker || new NielsenTracker();
    })();

    <script>
    (function (csnInsights) {

        function BITracker() {
            var biInfo = {};
            var cctnt = "";
            var requiredKeys = [];
                                        requiredKeys.push("make");
                    requiredKeys.push("model");
                    requiredKeys.push("badge");
                    requiredKeys.push("bodystyle");
                    requiredKeys.push("pricemin");
                    requiredKeys.push("pricemax");
                    requiredKeys.push("silotype");
                    requiredKeys.push("condition");
                    requiredKeys.push("sellertype");
                    requiredKeys.push("marca");
                    requiredKeys.push("modelo");
                    requiredKeys.push("distintivo");
                    requiredKeys.push("carroceria");
                    requiredKeys.push("segmento");
                    requiredKeys.push("preciomin");
                    requiredKeys.push("preciomax");
                    requiredKeys.push("tipo");

            var helperMethods = {
                getCommomParams: function(eventContext) {
                    var resultStr = "&trksrc=v2";
                    var evcontext = eventContext || { "metaData": {}};
                    var tnt = evcontext.metaData['tracktnt'] || '';
                    var cc = evcontext.metaData['trackcc'] || '';
                    var area = evcontext.metaData['contentgroup1'] || evcontext.metaData['contentGroup1'] ||'';
                    var pagetype = evcontext.metaData['contentgroup2'] || evcontext.metaData['contentGroup2'] || '';
                    var adtype = evcontext.metaData["adtype"] || '';
                 
                    if ((tnt) && (cc)) {
                        resultStr = resultStr + "&cc=" + cc + "&tnt=" + tnt;
                    } else {
                        if (area) {
                            resultStr = resultStr + "&area=" + area;
                        }
                        if (pagetype) {
                            resultStr = resultStr + "&pagetype=" + pagetype;
                        }
                        if (adtype) {
                            resultStr = resultStr + "&adtype=" + adtype;
                        }

                        resultStr = resultStr + cctnt;
                    }

                    return resultStr;
                }
            };
            function getSearchTimestamp() {
                var now = new Date();
                return now.getFullYear().toString() +
                    (now.getMonth() + 1) +
                    now.getDate() +
                    "-" +
                    now.getHours() +
                    now.getMinutes() +
                    now.getSeconds() +
                    "-" +
                    now.getMilliseconds();
            }
            function init(overridePageUrl, csnEventId) {
                var extUId = '';
                var kxuser = '';
                try {
                    if ((window.localStorage) && (window.localStorage['kxkuid'] || window.localStorage['kxuser'])) {
                        extUId = window.localStorage['kxkuid'];
                        kxuser = window.localStorage['kxuser'];
                    }
                } catch (e) { }

                var url = 'https://tracking.carsales.com.au' + '/fav.ico';

                url += "?SessionId=" + csnInsights.CurrentClient.getSessionId();

                url += "&ServerName=" + location.hostname;

                url += '&ExtUId=' + extUId;

                url += '&kxuser=' + kxuser;

                url += '&referrerUri=' + (document.referrer ? document.referrer.split('?')[0] : '');
                if (overridePageUrl) {
                    url += '&pg=' + overridePageUrl;
                }
                else {
                    url += '&pg=' + (location.pathname ? location.pathname.split('?')[0] : '');
                }


                url += '&UserId=' + (window.CsnInsights.memberTrackingId || '');

                if (window.CsnInsights.geoCountryCode) {
                    url += '&geocc=' + (window.CsnInsights.geoCountryCode || '');
                    }

                url += '&ts=' + new Date().getTime();

                visitorId = (CsnInsights.CurrentClient.getId() || '');
                upperCaseVisitorId = visitorId.toUpperCase();

                prevVisitorId = (CsnInsights.CurrentClient.getPrevId() || '');
                upperCasePrevVisitorId = prevVisitorId.toUpperCase();

                if (prevVisitorId != '') {
                    url += '&PrevVisitorId=' + upperCasePrevVisitorId;
                }

                url += '&VisitorId=' + upperCaseVisitorId;

                url += '&CsnEventId=' + (csnEventId || CsnInsights.LoadEventId);

                biInfo.url = url;
            };
            function addBodyStyleToUrl(bodyStyle, url, saveItem=false) {
                if(!saveItem){
                    return url + (bodyStyle ? ("&BodyStyle=" + bodyStyle):'');
                }
                return url + (bodyStyle ? ("&BodyStyle=" + bodyStyle) : '');
            };
            function thankyouPageHandler(eventContext) {
                var pageType = eventContext.metaData['contentgroup2']
                    || eventContext.metaData['contentGroup2']
                    || eventContext.metaData['pagetype']
                    || eventContext.metaData['pageType']
                    || '';
                if (pageType.toLowerCase() === 'thankyou') {
                    var networkId = eventContext.metaData['networkid'] || '';
                    var url = biInfo.url;

                    url += "&EventType=E";

                    if (eventContext.metaData['eventsource']) {
                        url += "&EventSource=" + eventContext.metaData['eventsource'];
                    }

                    url += '&NetworkId=' + networkId + helperMethods.getCommomParams(eventContext);
                    url = addBodyStyleToUrl(eventContext.metaData['bodystyle'], url);
                    var biDetails = new Image();
                    biDetails.style.height = "0";
                    biDetails.style.width = "0";
                    biDetails.style.opacity = "0";
                    biDetails.style.visibility = "hidden";
                    biDetails.src = url;
                    var $el = document.getElementById('bitracking');
                    if ($el) {
                        $el.appendChild(biDetails);
                    } else {
                        document.body.appendChild(biDetails);

                    }
                }
            };
            function detailsPageHandler(eventContext) {
                var pageType = eventContext.metaData['contentgroup2']
                    || eventContext.metaData['contentGroup2']
                    || eventContext.metaData['pagetype']
                    || eventContext.metaData['pageType']
                    || '';
                if (pageType.toLowerCase() === 'details' || pageType.toLowerCase() === 'story' ) {
                    var networkId = eventContext.metaData['networkid'] || eventContext.metaData['networkId'] || '';
                    var url = biInfo.url;

                    if (window.location.href.indexOf('gts=') > 0 ||
                        window.location.href.indexOf('gtssaleid=') > 0) {
                        url += "&EventType=GV&SaleID=" + networkId;
                    } else {
                        url += "&EventType=V";
                    }
                    if (eventContext.metaData['eventsource']) {
                        url += "&EventSource=" + eventContext.metaData['eventsource'];
                    }

                    url += '&NetworkId=' + networkId + helperMethods.getCommomParams(eventContext);
                    url = addBodyStyleToUrl(eventContext.metaData['bodystyle'], url);
                    var biDetails = new Image();
                    biDetails.style.height = "0";
                    biDetails.style.width = "0";
                    biDetails.style.opacity = "0";
                    biDetails.style.visibility = "hidden";
                    biDetails.src = url;
                    var $el = document.getElementById('bitracking');
                    if ($el) {
                        $el.appendChild(biDetails);
                    } else {
                         document.body.appendChild(biDetails);

                    }
                }

            };
            function saveItemEventHandler(eventContext, eventCategory, eventData, eventLabel, overridePageUrl) {

                if ((eventLabel || '').startsWith('save-item') || (eventLabel || '').startsWith('save_item')) {
                    if ((eventContext.memberTrackingId && eventContext.memberTrackingId.toString().length > 0) && eventContext.memberTrackingId !== '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000') {

                        var networkId = eventContext.metaData['networkid'] || eventContext.metaData['networkId'] || '';
                        if (networkId === '') {
                            try {
                                networkId = eventData["networkid"] || '';

                            } catch (e) {

                            } 
                        }
                        var isgts = ((eventData || {})['isgts'] || '') === "1";
                        var url = biInfo.url;
                        if (isgts === true || window.location.href.indexOf('gts=') > 0 ||
                            window.location.href.indexOf('gtssaleid=') > 0 || (overridePageUrl || '').indexOf('gtssaleid=') > 0) {
                            url += "&EventType=GSAV";
                        } else {
                            url += "&EventType=SAV";
                        }
                        if (eventContext.metaData['eventsource']) {
                            url += "&EventSource=" + eventContext.metaData['eventsource'];
                        }
                        url += '&NetworkId=' + networkId + helperMethods.getCommomParams(eventContext);
                        var pgtype = eventContext.metaData['contentgroup2'] || eventContext.metaData['contentGroup2']
                            || eventContext.metaData['pagetype'] || eventContext.metaData['pageType'] || '';
                        url += "&pagetype=" + pgtype ;
                        if (pgtype.toLowerCase() === 'story' || pgtype.toLowerCase() === 'details'){
                            url = addBodyStyleToUrl(eventContext.metaData['bodystyle'], url, saveItem=true);
                        }
                        else if (pgtype.toLowerCase() === 'listing'){
                            url = addBodyStyleToUrl(eventData['bodystyle'], url,  saveItem=true);
                        }
                        var area = eventContext.metaData['contentgroup1'] || eventContext.metaData['contentGroup1'] ||
                            eventContext.metaData['area'] || '';
                        url += "&area=" + area;

                        var biDetails = new Image();
                        biDetails.style.height = "0";
                        biDetails.style.width = "0";
                        biDetails.style.opacity = "0";
                        biDetails.style.visibility = "hidden";
                        biDetails.src = url;
                        var $el = document.getElementById('bitracking');
                        if ($el) {
                            $el.appendChild(biDetails);
                        } else {
                            document.body.appendChild(biDetails);

                        }

                    }
                }

            };
            function galleryPageHandler(eventContext) {

                var pageType = eventContext.metaData['contentgroup2']
                    || eventContext.metaData['contentGroup2']
                    || eventContext.metaData['pagetype']
                    || eventContext.metaData['pageType']
                    || '';
                if (pageType.toLowerCase() === 'gallery') {
                    var networkId = eventContext.metaData['networkid'] || eventContext.metaData['networkId'] || '';

                    var url = biInfo.url;

                    url += "&EventType=M";

                    if (window.location.href.indexOf('gts=') > 0 ||
                        window.location.href.indexOf('gtssaleid=') > 0) {
                        url += "&SaleID=" + networkId;
                    }

                    url += '&NetworkId=' + networkId + helperMethods.getCommomParams(eventContext);
                    url = addBodyStyleToUrl(eventContext.metaData['bodystyle'], url);
                    var biGallery = new Image();
                    biGallery.style.height = "0";
                    biGallery.style.width = "0";
                    biGallery.style.opacity = "0";
                    biGallery.style.visibility = "hidden";
                    biGallery.src = url;
                    var $el = document.getElementById('bitracking');
                    if ($el) {
                        $el.appendChild(biGallery);
                    } else {
                        document.body.appendChild(biGallery);

                    }
                }

            };
            function listingResultHandler(eventContext, searchResultsv2 = '') {

                var pageType = eventContext.metaData['contentgroup2']
                    || eventContext.metaData['contentGroup2']
                    || eventContext.metaData['pagetype']
                    || eventContext.metaData['pageType']
                    || '';

                if (pageType.toLowerCase() === 'listing' || (pageType.toLowerCase() === 'homepage' && searchResultsv2 !== '')) {
                    
                    var url = biInfo.url;
                    url += "&EventType=SR";
                    url += "&SearchTS=" + getSearchTimestamp();
                    url += "&SearchResultCount=" + (eventContext.metaData['listingresultcount'] || '');

                    if (pageType.toLowerCase() === 'listing') {

                        url += "&SearchItemsPerPage=" + (eventContext.metaData['itemsperpage'] || ''); /*itemsperpage will be supplied by the client*/

                        var searchParams = '';
                        for (var key in eventContext.metaData) {
                            if (requiredKeys.indexOf(key) > -1) {
                                if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(eventContext.metaData, key)) {
                                    searchParams += key + ':' + eventContext.metaData[key] + ';';
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        url += "&SearchParams=" + searchParams + helperMethods.getCommomParams(eventContext);
                    }
                    if (pageType.toLowerCase() === 'homepage') {
                        url += '&EventSource=myfeed';
                    }

                    var networkIdList = '';

                    var results;
                    if (eventContext.searchResults) {
                        results = eventContext.searchResults['results'];
                    }

                    if (results) {
                        url += "&NetworkIdList=" + results;
                    } else {

                        if (eventContext.searchResultsv2) {
                            if (searchResultsv2) {
                                results = searchResultsv2['Results'];
                            }
                            else {
                                results = eventContext.searchResultsv2['Results'];
                            }

                            results.forEach(function (result) {
                                networkIdList += result.Id + ',';
                            });

                            url += "&NetworkIdList=" + networkIdList;

                        }
                    }
                    var biListingResult = new Image();
                    biListingResult.style.height = "0";
                    biListingResult.style.width = "0";
                    biListingResult.style.opacity = "0";
                    biListingResult.style.visibility = "hidden";
                    biListingResult.src = url;
                    var $el = document.getElementById('bitracking');
                    if ($el) {
                        $el.appendChild(biListingResult);
                    } else {
                        document.body.appendChild(biListingResult);
                    }
                }
            };
            function gtsListingResultHandler(eventContext) {

                var pageType = eventContext.metaData['contentgroup2']
                    || eventContext.metaData['contentGroup2']
                    || eventContext.metaData['pagetype']
                    || eventContext.metaData['pageType']
                    || '';

                var gtsresultsv1;
                var gtsresultsv2;

                if(eventContext.searchResults){
                    gtsresultsv1 = eventContext.searchResults['gtsresults'];
                }

                if(!gtsresultsv1 && eventContext.searchResultsv2){
                    gtsresultsv2 =  eventContext.searchResultsv2['GtsResults'];
                }

                var hasGts = gtsresultsv1 || gtsresultsv2;

                if (pageType.toLowerCase() === 'listing' && hasGts) {

                    var url = biInfo.url;

                    url += "&EventType=GSR";

                    url += "&SearchTS=" + getSearchTimestamp();

                    url += "&SearchResultCount=" + (eventContext.metaData['listingresultcount'] || '');

                    url += "&SearchItemsPerPage=" + (eventContext.metaData['itemsperpage'] || ''); /*itemsperpage will be supplied by the client*/

                    var searchParams = '';
                    for (var key in eventContext.metaData) {
                        if (requiredKeys.indexOf(key) > -1) {
                            if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(eventContext.metaData, key)) {
                                searchParams += key + ':' + eventContext.metaData[key] + ';';
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    url += "&SearchParams=" + searchParams + helperMethods.getCommomParams(eventContext);

                    var networkIdList = '';

                    var gtsresults;

                    if (eventContext.searchResults) {
                        gtsresults = eventContext.searchResults['gtsresults'];
                    }

                    if (gtsresults) {
                        url += "&NetworkIdList=" + gtsresults;
                    } else {

                        if (eventContext.searchResultsv2) {
                            gtsresults = eventContext.searchResultsv2['GtsResults'];

                            gtsresults.forEach(function (gtsResult) {

                                networkIdList += gtsResult.Id + ',';
                            });

                            url += "&NetworkIdList=" + networkIdList;
                        }
                    }
                    var biGtsListingResult = new Image();
                    biGtsListingResult.style.height = "0";
                    biGtsListingResult.style.width = "0";
                    biGtsListingResult.style.opacity = "0";
                    biGtsListingResult.style.visibility = "hidden";
                    biGtsListingResult.src = url;
                    var $el = document.getElementById('bitracking');
                    if ($el) {
                        $el.appendChild(biGtsListingResult);
                    } else {
                        document.body.appendChild(biGtsListingResult);

                    }
                    }
            };

            function whatsAppClickHandler(eventContext, eventCategory, eventData, eventLabel, overridePageUrl) {
                var url = biInfo.url;

                if (eventLabel.indexOf("whatsapp_enquiry") > -1) {
                    var networkId = eventContext.metaData['networkid'] || '';
                    url += "&EventType=WAPCLKT";
                    url += '&NetworkId=' + networkId + helperMethods.getCommomParams(eventContext);

                    var biWhatsApp = new Image();
                    biWhatsApp.style.height = "0";
                    biWhatsApp.style.width = "0";
                    biWhatsApp.style.opacity = "0";
                    biWhatsApp.style.visibility = "hidden";
                    biWhatsApp.src = url;
                    var $el = document.getElementById('bitracking');
                    if ($el) {
                        $el.appendChild(biWhatsApp);
                    } else {
                        document.body.appendChild(biWhatsApp);
                    }
                }
            };

            function callConnectClickHandler(eventContext, eventCategory, eventData, eventLabel, overridePageUrl) {
                /*CCCLKT*/
                var url = biInfo.url;
                if ((eventCategory.indexOf("enquiry_call") > -1) && eventContext.metaData['callconnect'] == 'true') {
                    var networkId = eventContext.metaData['networkid'] || '';
                    url += "&EventType=CCONCLKT";
                    url += '&NetworkId=' + networkId + helperMethods.getCommomParams(eventContext);

                    var biPhoneReveal = new Image();
                    biPhoneReveal.style.height = "0";
                    biPhoneReveal.style.width = "0";
                    biPhoneReveal.style.opacity = "0";
                    biPhoneReveal.style.visibility = "hidden";
                    biPhoneReveal.src = url;
                    var $el = document.getElementById('bitracking');
                    if ($el) {
                        $el.appendChild(biPhoneReveal);
                    } else {
                        document.body.appendChild(biPhoneReveal);
                    }
                }
            };

            function nonCallConnectClickHandler(eventContext, eventCategory, eventData, eventLabel, overridePageUrl) {
                /*NCCCLKT*/
                var url = biInfo.url;
                if ((eventCategory.indexOf("enquiry_call") > -1) && eventContext.metaData['callconnect'] == 'false') {
                    var networkId = eventContext.metaData['networkid'] || '';
                    url += "&EventType=NCCONCLKT";
                    url += '&NetworkId=' + networkId + helperMethods.getCommomParams(eventContext);

                    var biPhoneReveal = new Image();
                    biPhoneReveal.style.height = "0";
                    biPhoneReveal.style.width = "0";
                    biPhoneReveal.style.opacity = "0";
                    biPhoneReveal.style.visibility = "hidden";
                    biPhoneReveal.src = url;
                    var $el = document.getElementById('bitracking');
                    if ($el) {
                        $el.appendChild(biPhoneReveal);
                    } else {
                        document.body.appendChild(biPhoneReveal);
                    }
                }
            };

            function phoneRevealClickHandler(eventContext, eventCategory, eventData, eventLabel, overridePageUrl) {
                var url = biInfo.url;
                if (eventLabel.indexOf("reveal_phone") > -1) {
                    var networkId = eventContext.metaData['networkid'] || '';
                    url += "&EventType=RPHCLKT";
                    url += '&NetworkId=' + networkId + helperMethods.getCommomParams(eventContext);

                    var biPhoneReveal = new Image();
                    biPhoneReveal.style.height = "0";
                    biPhoneReveal.style.width = "0";
                    biPhoneReveal.style.opacity = "0";
                    biPhoneReveal.style.visibility = "hidden";
                    biPhoneReveal.src = url;
                    var $el = document.getElementById('bitracking');
                    if ($el) {
                        $el.appendChild(biPhoneReveal);
                    } else {
                        document.body.appendChild(biPhoneReveal);
                    }
                }
            };

            var getHandlers = function () {
                return [listingResultHandler, gtsListingResultHandler, detailsPageHandler, galleryPageHandler, thankyouPageHandler];
            };

            var getClickHandlers = function () {
                return [phoneRevealClickHandler, whatsAppClickHandler, saveItemEventHandler, callConnectClickHandler, nonCallConnectClickHandler];
            };

            return {
                sendPageView: function (eventContextmetaData, overridePageUrl, variantTestContext, searchResultsV2, nonInteraction, csnEventId) {
                    init(overridePageUrl, csnEventId);
                    var eventContext = window.CsnInsights || {};
                    if (typeof (eventContextmetaData) !== 'undefined') {
                        if (typeof (eventContextmetaData.metaData) !== 'undefined') {
                            eventContext.metaData = eventContextmetaData.metaData;
                        }
                        else {
                            eventContext.metaData = eventContextmetaData;
                        }
                    }

                    var handlers = getHandlers();

                    for (var i = 0; i < handlers.length; i++) {
                        try {
                            handlers[i](eventContext);
                        } catch (e) { }
                    }
                },
                sendClick: function (eventContextmetaData, eventCategory, eventLabel, eventData, overridePageUrl, variantTestContext, nonInteraction, csnEventId) {
                    init(overridePageUrl, csnEventId);
                    var eventContext = window.CsnInsights || {};
                    if (typeof (eventContextmetaData) !== 'undefined') {
                        if (typeof (eventContextmetaData.metaData) !== 'undefined') {
                            eventContext.metaData = eventContextmetaData.metaData;
                        }
                        else {
                            eventContext.metaData = eventContextmetaData;
                        }
                    }
                    var clickHandlers = getClickHandlers();
                    for (var i = 0; i < clickHandlers.length; i++) {
                        try{
                            clickHandlers[i](eventContext, eventCategory, eventData, eventLabel, overridePageUrl);
                        } catch (e) { }
                    }
                },
                sendEvent: function (eventContextmetaData, eventCategory, eventLabel, eventAction, eventData, overridePageUrl, variantTestContext, searchResultsV2, nonInteraction, csnEventId) {
                    init(overridePageUrl, csnEventId);
                    var eventContext = window.CsnInsights || {};
                    if (typeof (eventContextmetaData) !== 'undefined') {
                        if (typeof (eventContextmetaData.metaData) !== 'undefined') {
                            eventContext.metaData = eventContextmetaData.metaData;
                        }
                        else {
                            eventContext.metaData = eventContextmetaData;
                        }
                    }
                    listingResultHandler(eventContext, searchResultsV2);                              
                }
            };
        };
        window.BITracker = window.BITracker || new BITracker();
        if ((CsnInsights.fireOnLoad === undefined) || (CsnInsights.fireOnLoad !== false)) {
            if (CsnInsights.metaData) {
                window.BITracker.sendPageView(CsnInsights.metaData, null, CsnInsights.LoadEventId);
            }
        };

    })(CsnInsights);

    window.CsnInsights.AppNexusHelper = {
        sendPageView: function (eventData, overridePageUrl) {

            var pageType = (((CsnInsights || {}).metaData || {}).contentgroup2 || "").toLowerCase();
            var area = (((CsnInsights || {}).metaData || {}).contentgroup1 || "").toLowerCase();

            if (area === "instant-offer" && pageType === "/instant-offer/offer-accepted/") {
                var adImg = document.createElement("img");
                adImg.setAttribute('src', 'https://secure.adnxs.com/px?id=1118976&t=2');
                adImg.setAttribute('alt', 'na');
                adImg.setAttribute('height', '1px');
                adImg.setAttribute('width', '1px');
                document.body.appendChild(adImg);
            }
        }
    };
    if ((CsnInsights.fireOnLoad === undefined) || (CsnInsights.fireOnLoad !== false)) {
        window.CsnInsights.AppNexusHelper.sendPageView();
    }

    (function () {

                    window.CsnInsights.AppNexusHelper.sendPageView(eventContextmetaData, overridePageUrl);

</script>   <script>
    (function ClickTracker() {
        var ignoreForLowerCaseList = ['data-webm-recommendationid', 'data-webm-slotid'];
        var methods =
        {
            isValueValid : function(value){
                return (typeof (value) !== 'undefined') &&  (value !== null);
            },
            tryGetAttributeValue: function(domElement, key)
            {
                var attributeValue = domElement.getAttribute(key);
                var isKeyInIgnoreList = methods.isValueInArray(ignoreForLowerCaseList, key);
                if (methods.isValueValid(attributeValue) && !isKeyInIgnoreList)
                    attributeValue = attributeValue.toLowerCase();

                return attributeValue;

            },
            isValueInArray: function (arr, value) {
                var found = false;
                if (arr instanceof Array) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
                        if (arr[i] === value) {
                            found = true;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
                return found;
            },
            tryGetValueFromClickElementAttributes : function(domElement){
                var textContent;
                if (typeof(domElement) !== 'undefined'
                    && domElement.tagName.toLowerCase() ==  '') /* Extend for elements like a,img if needed*/
                {
                    textContent = domElement.textContent;
                    if (!methods.isValueValid(textContent))
                    {
                        textContent = methods.tryGetAttributeValue(domElement, 'href');
                    }

                }
                return textContent;
            },
            getClickValueInParents: function(domElement, levels)
            {
                var thisDomElement = domElement;
                var clickValueFound = false;
                var clickValue = undefined;
                while((!clickValue) && typeof(thisDomElement) !== 'undefined' && (thisDomElement)
                    && thisDomElement.tagName.toLowerCase() !=  'body'
                    && (levels > 0))
                {
                    var clickValue = methods.tryGetAttributeValue(thisDomElement,'data-webm-clickvalue');
                    if ((typeof (clickValue) === 'undefined') ||
                        (clickValue === null) || (clickValue === ''))
                    {
                        thisDomElement = thisDomElement.parentElement;
                        levels = levels - 1;
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        clickValueFound = true;
                        clickValue = clickValue.toLowerCase();
                    }
                }
                return	clickValue;
            },
            getClickValueDataInParents: function (domElement, levels) {
                var ret = {};
                var thisDomElement = domElement;
                var clickValue = undefined;
                while ((!clickValue) && typeof (thisDomElement) !== 'undefined' && (thisDomElement)
                    && thisDomElement.tagName.toLowerCase() != 'body'
                    && (levels > 0)) {
                    var clickValue = methods.tryGetAttributeValue(thisDomElement, 'data-webm-clickvalue');
                    if ((typeof (clickValue) === 'undefined') ||
                        (clickValue === null) || (clickValue === '')) {
                        thisDomElement = thisDomElement.parentElement;
                        levels = levels - 1;
                    }
                    else {
                        ret = methods.getStructureFromDomElement(thisDomElement);
                    }
                }
                return ret;
            },
            getStructureFromDomElement: function (domElement) {
                var ret = {};
                var value = methods.tryGetAttributeValue(domElement, 'data-webm-clickvalue');
                ret["clickValue"] = value.toLowerCase();
                for (var i = 0; i < domElement.attributes.length; i++) {
                    var attrib = domElement.attributes[i];
                    var name = attrib.name;
                    if (attrib && (name.indexOf("data-webm-") === 0)) {
                        ret[attrib.name.replace('data-webm-', '')] = methods.tryGetAttributeValue(domElement, attrib.name);
                    }
                }
                return ret;
            },
            getClickCategory: function(domElement)
            {
                /*Search for datawebmsection*/
                var thisDomElement = domElement;
                var categoryfound = false;
                var category = undefined;

                /*check for category attribute in parents.*/
                while(!categoryfound && typeof(thisDomElement) !== 'undefined'
                    && thisDomElement.tagName.toLowerCase() !=  'body')
                {
                    var categoryValue = methods.tryGetAttributeValue(thisDomElement,'data-webm-section');
                    if ((typeof (categoryValue) === 'undefined') ||
                        (categoryValue === null))
                    {
                        thisDomElement = thisDomElement.parentElement;
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        categoryfound = true;
                        category = categoryValue.toLowerCase();
                    }

                }

                if (typeof(category) === 'undefined')
                {
                    category = 'UnCategorized';
                }

                return category;

            },
            getClickLabel: function(domElement)
            {
                var clickLabel = undefined;

                /*Try to get attribute value for the current element	*/
                var value = methods.tryGetAttributeValue(domElement, 'data-webm-clickvalue');

                if (methods.isValueValid(value))
                {
                    return value;
                }
                value = methods.getClickValueInParents(domElement, 10);
                if (methods.isValueValid(value))
                {
                    return value;
                }
                /*If the current dom is clickable(eg. anchor, then use the target as click value)*/
                value = methods.tryGetValueFromClickElementAttributes(domElement);
                if (methods.isValueValid(value))
                {
                    return value;
                }

            },
            getClickElementData: function(domElement) {
                var clickLabel = undefined;
                value = methods.getClickValueDataInParents(domElement, 10);
                if (methods.isValueValid(value)) {
                    return value;
                }
                /*If the current dom is clickable(eg. anchor, then use the target as click value)*/
                value = methods.tryGetValueFromClickElementAttributes(domElement);
                if (methods.isValueValid(value)) {
                    return value;
                }
            },
            clickTrackingHandler : function	(element) {

                if (typeof(element) ==='undefined' || typeof(element.target) ==='undefined' )
                    return;

                if (typeof (CsnInsightsEventTracker) === 'undefined'
                    || typeof (CsnInsightsEventTracker.sendClick) !== 'function')
                    return;

                /*read Section attribute*/
                var clickLabelData = methods.getClickElementData(element.target);
                if (methods.isValueValid(clickLabelData.clickValue)){
                    var clickCategory = methods.getClickCategory(element.target);
                    var eventContext = window.CsnInsights || {};                   
                    CsnInsightsEventTracker.sendClick(eventContext.metaData, clickCategory, clickLabelData.clickValue, clickLabelData, undefined);
                }
            }
        };
        window.CsnInsights = window.CsnInsights || {};
        if ((CsnInsights.disableAttributeClickTracking === undefined) || (CsnInsights.disableAttributeClickTracking !== true))
        {
            if (document.addEventListener)
            {
                document.addEventListener('click',methods.clickTrackingHandler);
            }
            else if (document.attachEvent)
            {
                document.attachEvent('click',methods.clickTrackingHandler);
            }
        }

    })();

</script><script>
 /* GA Insights Event Tracker Script */
(function() {
     function CsnInsightsHelper() {
         var methods = {
             setSessionCookie: function(cname, cvalue) {
                 document.cookie = cname + '=' + cvalue + ';path=/';
             },
             setCookie: function(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
                 var d = new Date();
                 d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
                 var expires = 'expires = ' + d.toUTCString();
                 document.cookie = cname + '=' + cvalue + ';' + expires + ';path=/';
             },
             getCookieValue: function(cname) {
                 var cookiesString = document.cookie || '';
                 var cookiesArr = cookiesString.split('; ');
                 for (var i = 0; i < cookiesArr.length; i++) {
                     var cookieStr = cookiesArr[i];
                     var index = cookieStr.indexOf('=');
                     if (index < 1) {
                         return undefined;
                     }
                     var cookieName = decodeURIComponent(cookieStr.substr(0, index));
                     if (cookieName === cname) {
                         return decodeURIComponent(cookieStr.substr(index + 1));
                     }
                 }
                 return undefined;
             },
             calculateScrollPercent: function(absScrollPercent) {
                 var scrollPercentCategory = 0;
                 if (absScrollPercent >= 25 && absScrollPercent <= 50)
                     scrollPercentCategory = 25;
                 else if (absScrollPercent >= 50 && absScrollPercent <= 75)
                     scrollPercentCategory = 50;
                 else if (absScrollPercent >= 75 && absScrollPercent < 99)
                     scrollPercentCategory = 75;
                 else if (absScrollPercent >= 99)
                     scrollPercentCategory = 100;

                 return scrollPercentCategory;
             },
             getScrollText: function(absScrollPercent) {
             var scrolltext = "Less than 25%";
             if (absScrollPercent == 100)
                 scrolltext = "Viewed 100 %";
             else if (absScrollPercent >= 25)
                 scrolltext = "Viewed more than Or equal to" + absScrollPercent + " %";
             return scrolltext;
             },
             isIPad: function (fieldsObject) {                 
                const uAgent = window.navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
                const isIPad = (uAgent.indexOf('ipad') > -1 || uAgent.indexOf('mac') > -1) &&
                    window.navigator.maxTouchPoints && window.navigator.maxTouchPoints > 0 &&
                    'ontouchend' in document;

                if (isIPad === true) {
                    /* convert json string to object and add a new key/value then convert it back to json string*/
                    var cd11 = JSON.parse(fieldsObject['dimension11']);
                    cd11['isipad'] = true;
                    fieldsObject['dimension11'] = JSON.stringify(cd11);
                }
                return fieldsObject;               
             }
         };
        return {
            setCookie : function(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
                methods.setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays)
            },
            getCookieValue : function(cname) {
                return methods.getCookieValue(cname);
            },
            calculateScrollPercent: function (absScrollPercent) {
                return methods.calculateScrollPercent(absScrollPercent);
            },
            getScrollText: function (absScrollPercent) {
                return methods.getScrollText(absScrollPercent);
            },
            isIPad: function(fieldsObject) {
                return methods.isIPad(fieldsObject);
            }
         }

    };

    window.csnInsightsHelper = window.csnInsightsHelper || new CsnInsightsHelper();


    function GAEventTracker()

    var that = this;
    var collatecustomTagsFromBaseIndex = function (unMappedDimensions, baseIndex) {
        var tempArr = {};
        if (unMappedDimensions["virtualcaravanshow"] !==  "undefined") {
            tempArr["virtualcaravanshow"] = unMappedDimensions["virtualcaravanshow"];
            unMappedDimensions["virtualcaravanshow"] = undefined;
        }
        if (unMappedDimensions["onlineexpo"] !== "undefined") {
            tempArr["onlineexpo"] = unMappedDimensions["onlineexpo"];
            unMappedDimensions["onlineexpo"] = undefined;
        }
        if (unMappedDimensions["descuentosonline"] !== "undefined") {
            tempArr["descuentosonline"] = unMappedDimensions["descuentosonline"];
            unMappedDimensions["descuentosonline"] = undefined;
        }

        var unmappedDimensionBase = baseIndex;
        var unMappedDimensionsKeys = Object.keys(unMappedDimensions);
        if (unMappedDimensionsKeys.length > 0) {
            CsnInsights.unMappedDimensionsErr = unMappedDimensionsKeys;
            for (var i = 0; i < unMappedDimensionsKeys.length; i++) {
                if (typeof (unMappedDimensions[unMappedDimensionsKeys[i]]) !== 'undefined') {
                    if (((i + 1) % 5) === 0) {
                        tempArr[unMappedDimensionsKeys[i]] = unMappedDimensions[unMappedDimensionsKeys[i]].toString().toLowerCase().substring(0, 50);
                        unmappedDimensionIndex = unmappedDimensionIndex + 1;
                        CsnInsights.fieldsObject['dimension' + (unmappedDimensionBase + unmappedDimensionIndex)] = JSON.stringify(tempArr);
                        tempArr = {};
                    }
                    else {
                        tempArr[unMappedDimensionsKeys[i]] = unMappedDimensions[unMappedDimensionsKeys[i]].toString().toLowerCase().substring(0, 50);
                    }
                }
            }
            if (Object.keys(tempArr).length > 0) {
                unmappedDimensionIndex = unmappedDimensionIndex + 1;
                CsnInsights.fieldsObject['dimension' + (unmappedDimensionBase + unmappedDimensionIndex)] = JSON.stringify(tempArr);
            }
        }

        var methods = {
            externalid_dim : 'dimension9',

            collectTags: function (eventContext) {
                if ((typeof (eventContext) !== 'undefined') && (typeof (eventContext.metaData) !== 'undefined')
                    && (eventContext) && (eventContext.customMappings)) {
                    var metaDataKeys = Object.keys(eventContext.metaData);
                    var unMappedDimensions = {};
                    var seller_review_info = {};
                    for (var i = 0; i < metaDataKeys.length; i++) {
                        if (eventContext.metaData[metaDataKeys[i]] === undefined) {
                            continue;
                        }
                        if (typeof (eventContext.customMappings[metaDataKeys[i].toLowerCase()]) !== 'undefined') {
                            if (eventContext.customMappings[metaDataKeys[i].toLowerCase()].toLowerCase().indexOf('metric') === 0) {
                                CsnInsights.fieldsObject[eventContext.customMappings[metaDataKeys[i].toLowerCase()]] =
                                    (eventContext.metaData[metaDataKeys[i]] || '').toString().replace(/,/g, '');
                            }
                            else {
                                CsnInsights.fieldsObject[eventContext.customMappings[metaDataKeys[i].toLowerCase()]] = (eventContext.metaData[metaDataKeys[i]] || '').toString().toLowerCase();
                            }
                        } else {
                            if (metaDataKeys[i].toLowerCase().indexOf('contentgroup') === 0) {
                                CsnInsights.fieldsObject[metaDataKeys[i]] = eventContext.metaData[metaDataKeys[i]].toLowerCase();
                            }
                            else if (metaDataKeys[i].toLowerCase().indexOf('area') === 0
                                || metaDataKeys[i].toLowerCase().indexOf('pagetype') === 0
                                || metaDataKeys[i].toLowerCase().indexOf('sellertype') === 0)
                            {
                                CsnInsights.fieldsObject[metaDataKeys[i]] = eventContext.metaData[metaDataKeys[i]].toLowerCase();
                            } 
                            else if (metaDataKeys[i].toLowerCase().indexOf('sellerreview_averagerating') === 0
                                || metaDataKeys[i].toLowerCase().indexOf('sellerreview_totalreviews') === 0
                                || metaDataKeys[i].toLowerCase().indexOf('sellerreview_ratingprovider') === 0) {                              
                                    seller_review_info[metaDataKeys[i].toLowerCase()] = (eventContext.metaData[metaDataKeys[i]] || '').toString().toLowerCase();                            
                            }
                            else {
                                if (metaDataKeys[i].toLowerCase() === 'eventdata') {
                                    try {       
                                        eventd = (eventContext.metaData[metaDataKeys[i]] || "");
                                        if (JSON.stringify(eventd) !== "{}") {
                                            CsnInsights.fieldsObject['dimension83'] = eventd.toString().toLowerCase();
                                        }                                   
                                        
                                    } catch (e) { }
                                }
                                else {
                                    unMappedDimensions[metaDataKeys[i].toLowerCase()] = (eventContext.metaData[metaDataKeys[i]] || '').toString().toLowerCase();
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }


                    if ( Object.keys(seller_review_info).length > 0 ) {
                        CsnInsights.fieldsObject['dimension104'] = JSON.stringify(seller_review_info);
                    }

                    collatecustomTagsFromBaseIndex(unMappedDimensions, 10);
                    if ((eventContext.memberTrackingId && eventContext.memberTrackingId.toString().length > 0)) {
                        if (eventContext.memberTrackingId !== '00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000') {
                            CsnInsights.fieldsObject['userId'] = CsnInsights.memberTrackingId;
                        }

                        CsnInsights.fieldsObject[this.membertrackingid_dim] = CsnInsights.memberTrackingId;
                    };
                };
            },
            updateDataParamKeys: function (eventContext, fieldsObject) {
                if ((eventContext) && (eventContext.metaData) && (fieldsObject)) {
                    var metadataKeys = Object.keys(eventContext.metaData);
                    var data = '';
                    var excludedMetaDatakeys = ['contentgroup1', 'contentgroup2', 'contentgroup3', 'service', 'area', 'pagetype'];
                    for (var i = 0; i < metadataKeys.length; i++) {
                        if (excludedMetaDatakeys.indexOf((metadataKeys[i] || '').toLowerCase()) == -1) {
                            data = data + (metadataKeys[i] || '').toLowerCase() + ',';
                        }
                    }
                    if (data) {
                        fieldsObject[this.dataparams_dim] = data.substring(0, 150);
                    }
                }
            },
            getItemCategory: function (itemId) {
                if (!itemId) {
                    return '';
                }
                if (itemId.substr(0, 3).toLowerCase() === 'sse') {
                    return 'private';
                }
                else {
                    return 'dealer';
                }

            },
            getCustomUrl: function (eventContext, eventUrl) {
                var customUrl = undefined;
                if ((eventUrl !== undefined) && (eventUrl !== '') && (eventUrl.indexOf('/') === 0)) {
                    customUrl = eventUrl;
                }
                if ((eventContext.overridePageUrl !== undefined) && (eventContext.overridePageUrl.indexOf('/') === 0)) {
                    customUrl = eventContext.overridePageUrl;
                } else {
                    var pageType = eventContext.metaData['contentgroup2'];
                    if (pageType === undefined) {
                        pageType = eventContext.metaData['contentGroup2'];
                    }
                    if (pageType === undefined) {
                        pageType = eventContext.metaData['pagetype'];
                    }
                    if (pageType === undefined) {
                        pageType = eventContext.metaData['pageType'];
                    }
                    if ((pageType !== undefined) &&
                        ((pageType.toLowerCase() == 'details')
                            || (pageType.toLowerCase() == 'gallery')
                            || (pageType.toLowerCase() == 'enquiryform')
                            || (pageType.toLowerCase() == 'thankyou')))
                    {
                        var contentGroup1 = eventContext.metaData['contentgroup1'];
                        if (contentGroup1 === undefined) {
                            contentGroup1 = eventContext.metaData['contentGroup1'];
                        }
                        if (contentGroup1 === undefined) {
                            contentGroup1 = eventContext.metaData['area'];
                        }
                        if (contentGroup1 === undefined) {
                            contentGroup1 = 'unknown';
                        }
                        customUrl = '/' + contentGroup1.toLowerCase().replace(/ /g, '_') + '/' + pageType.toLowerCase();
                    }
                }
                return customUrl;
            },
            setpageTypeIfApplicable: function (fieldsObject, customPageUrl) {
                if (((fieldsObject['contentGroup2'] === undefined) || (fieldsObject['contentGroup2'] === ''))
                        &&
                    ((fieldsObject['pagetype'] === undefined) || (fieldsObject['pagetype'] === ''))) {
                    if ((fieldsObject['contentGroup1'] !== undefined && fieldsObject['contentGroup1'].toLowerCase() === 'homepage')
                        ||

                        fieldsObject['contentGroup2'] = fieldsObject['contentGroup1'];
                        if (fieldsObject['contentGroup2'] === undefined) {
                            fieldsObject['contentGroup2'] = fieldsObject['area'];
                        }
                    } else {
                        if ((customPageUrl === undefined) || (!customPageUrl.indexOf('/') === 0)) {
                            fieldsObject['contentGroup2'] = location.pathname;
                        }
                        else {
                            fieldsObject['contentGroup2'] = customPageUrl;
                        }
                    }
                }
            },
            setVariantTestTags: function (fieldsObject, variantTestContext) {

            collectExtTags: function (csnEventId) {

                        extIds1['csncidcf'] = window.CsnInsightsHelper.getCookieValue('csncidcf');
                    }

                try {

                try {
